***гипсовый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гипсовый.html>ги́псовый</a> (13440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гипс.html>гипс</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gips</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гипсовый.html>ги́псовый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gípsovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gypsum; gypseous

***гиря.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гиря.html>ги́ря</a> (11082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Old Russian гыря, Bulgarian гiря.
Vasmer connects it  to the root of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">гвор</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gvor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> "bladder, tumor",
ultimately PIE <span class="Latinx" lang="ine-pro">*gʷreh₂-</span> "heavy". The phonology is difficult and may show Iranian influence (Indo-Iranian <span class="Latinx" lang="iir-pro">*Gr̥Húš</span>, modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">گران</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gerân</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> "heavy").
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Iron_16kg.jpg/220px-Iron_16kg.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="225" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Iron_16kg.jpg/330px-Iron_16kg.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Iron_16kg.jpg/440px-Iron_16kg.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1292" data-file-height="1320" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:гиря.html>ги́ря</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гиря.html>ги́ря</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gírja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гиря.html>ги́ри</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гиря.html>ги́ри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гиря.html>ги́рь</a></b>)

<ol><li>weight <i>for measuring</i></li>

***глава.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>глава́</a> (508)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>глава́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glava</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golva</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*galˀwā́ˀ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golová</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the regular East Slavic reflex.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>глава́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glavá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>главы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>гла́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>гла́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>head, top, summit</li>
<li>cupola, dome</li>
<li>chapter, section <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a book</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chief <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on a shield</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>глава́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glavá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>главы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>гла́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>гла́в</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:главарь.html>глава́рь</a> (9482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>глава́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glavá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́рь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-árʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главарь.html>глава́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glavárʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главарь.html>главаря́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главарь.html>главари́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главарь.html>главаре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>leader (e.g. of a gang); ringleader; chieftain</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:главенствовать.html>главе́нствовать</a> (26322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">главе́нство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glavénstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главенствовать.html>главе́нствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glavénstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to lead, to dominate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>гора́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:главенствовать.html>главе́нствует</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окружающее.html>окружа́ющей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>землёй</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gorá <b>glavénstvujet</b> nad okružájuščej zemljój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the mountain <b>dominates</b> the surrounding land</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to prevail</li></ol>

***главк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:главк.html>главк</a> (12532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главный.html>гла́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комитет.html>комите́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glávnyj komitét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главк.html>главк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glavk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главк.html>гла́вка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главк.html>гла́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главк.html>гла́вков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>central administrative board, central directorate, major committee</li></ol>

<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главнокомандующий.html>главнокома́ндующий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glavnokomándujuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главк.html>главко́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glavkóm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главком.html>главко́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главком.html>главко́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главком.html>главко́мов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:главный.html>гла́вный</a> (197)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>глава́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glavá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главный.html>гла́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glávnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)главне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)главне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:главный.html>гла́вный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>chief, leading, main</li>
<li>principal</li>
<li>central, head, senior</li>
<li>core</li></ol>

***глагол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> (14503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">глаголъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glagolŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <i class="Glag mention" lang="cu">ⰳⰾⰰⰳⱁⰾⱏ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glagolŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golgolъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">speech, word</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Displaced the native Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*гологол</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*gologol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, still found in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">голого́лить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gologólitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glagól</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">глаго́льный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> verb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> word; speech
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vasily_Rozanov" class="extiw" title="w:Vasily Rozanov">Василий Розанов</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:опавший.html>Опа́вшие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>ли́стья</a></cite>, box 2:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">испове́дывал <a href = vnd.unilang:краткий.html>кра́тко</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>Жду́т</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доход.html>дохо́ды</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>Так</a> „быт“ <a href = vnd.unilang:мешаться.html>меша́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небесный.html>небе́сным</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лом</a></b>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забывать.html>забыва́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быт.html>бы́те</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:слушать.html>слу́шая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотря́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быт.html>быт</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вспомнить.html>вспо́мни</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:однако.html>одна́ко</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ispovédyval krátko. Ždut. Slúžba i doxódy. Tak „byt“ mešájetsja s nebésnym <b>glagólom</b>, — i ne zabyváj o býte, slúšaja <b>glagól</b>, a, smotrjá na byt, vspómni, što ty, odnáko, slýšal i <b>glagóly</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He confessed shortly. They’re waiting. Service and revenue. So “life” mingles with the heavenly <b>word</b>—and don’t forget about life while listening to the <b>word</b>, and, looking at life, remember that you, however, have also heard the <b>word</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***гладить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гладить.html>гла́дить</a> (4229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гладить.html>гла́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gláditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погладить.html>погла́дить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to iron, to press (clothes)</li>
<li>to pet (animals, etc.)</li>
<li>to stroke, to caress</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гладкий.html>гла́дкий</a> (3602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gladъkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гладкий.html>гла́дкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gládkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)гла́же</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">гладча́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>smooth</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> well-fed</li></ol>

***глаз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a> (78)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">глазъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glazŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ball, eye</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*glazъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ball</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*g(ʰ)el-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">round, spherical, stone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glaz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>гла́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>eye</li>
<li>eyesight</li>
<li>view, opinion</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Note on irregular forms — <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glazá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is actually an old nominative dual form. The genitive plural in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glaz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is also an archaic form.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазок</a> (2813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glaz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glazók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>гла́зки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>гла́зок</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glaz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: little eye
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>гла́зки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stróitʹ <b>glázki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">make eyes at</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glazók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>eye spot, globule
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазо́к</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жир.html>жи́ра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суп.html>су́пе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Glazók</b> žíra v súpe</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A globule of fat on soup.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reproductive bud on a vegetable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картофельный.html>карто́фельный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазо́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kartófelʹnyj <b>glazók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Potato eye.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">horticulture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(in rural areas)</i> kidney-shaped scion cut from a plant and grafted onto rootstock</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lentigo or pigmented spot (in the coloration of insects, birds, plants); circle or dot in the design on a fabric
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:павлиний.html>Павли́ний</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазо́к</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвосте́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pavlinij <b>glazók</b> na xvosté</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eye on a peacock’s tailfeather.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> eyelet for threading the warp on a loom</li>
<li>eyehole, peephole, spyhole, or optical device for seeing through a wall or door
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дверной.html>дверно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:глазок.html>глазо́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dvernój <b>glazók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">peephole.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***глас.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глас.html>глас</a> (17259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">гласъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glasŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, not exhibiting pleophony as opposed to the inherited doublet <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gólos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глас.html>глас</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glas</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глас.html>гла́са</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гласный.html>гла́сный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> voice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:глас.html>глас</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>glas</b> naróda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">vox populi, the voice of the people</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:глас.html>глас</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопиющий.html>вопию́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустыня.html>пусты́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>glas</b> vopijúščevo v pustýne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">voice of him who is crying in the wilderness</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
